# Surrenderless — project state (source of truth)

This document aligns Cursor, ChatGPT, and humans on **product intent**, **current reality**, and **where to invest**. It describes the repo as of its last update; verify against code when in doubt.

---

## 1. True product goal

**Surrenderless is a chat-first action assistant.** The user should eventually **only chat** with Surrenderless — not manually hop across forms, tabs, and external sites as the primary experience. The user **chats**; the app:

- Gathers facts **conversationally**
- **Structures** the case
- **Collects and organizes** proof (screenshots, receipts, emails, and similar — tied to the case in-app)
- **Prepares** submissions, messages, and complaints for review (in-app previews and drafts today; more automation later where feasible)
- Gets **approval**
- **Submits or queues** actions when technically (and legally) possible
- **Tracks** confirmations, filings, and follow-ups
- **Carries** the issue from beginning to end

Existing **`/justice/*`** pages (intake form, evidence page, prep surfaces, etc.) are **interim scaffolding** toward that single conversational shell — not the final product shape.

Anything that permanently treats “open another tab and paste into a government form” as the final experience is **out of scope for the long-term product**, even if it is useful as an interim step.

---

## 2. Current reality

The shipped experience is **still a multi-page Consumer Justice case-management scaffold** (many prep surfaces and manual filing paths), but **navigation across hub, preview, plan, and prep surfaces now promotes AI conversational chat intake first** toward the long-term **chat-first action** goal (§1): describe the issue once in chat, structure the case, review a submission preview, approve, then follow evidence, filings, tasks, and plan guidance inside the app (filing/queueing only where feasible today; much remains manual prep and external filing).


- **Stack:** Next.js (App Router), TypeScript, **Clerk** (auth), **Supabase** (persistence via service-role API routes), **REST API routes**, **session/local storage** for active case + timeline mirror.
- **UX:** Multi-page **justice** routes (`/justice/*`): **`/justice`** workspace hub (thin landing); **primary chat intake** — **AI conversational** intake at **`/justice/chat-ai`** (§2; hub/header **Chat intake** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; preview empty-state/footer **Chat intake** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; §2 **Justice-wide navigation alignment**); **step-by-step scripted** intake at **`/justice/chat`** (labeled **Step-by-step chat** where linked; **unchanged** scripted Q&A); **structured form** intake at **`/justice/intake`** (labeled **Structured form** / **Edit structured form** where linked; loads saved answers for direct field edit); action plan; **`/justice/preview`** (in-app **submission draft preview**: deterministic text from **`buildSubmissionDraftPreview.ts`** remains **source of truth / fallback**; optional **AI-assisted** draft via signed-in **`POST /api/justice/preview-draft`** (Clerk **`getUserOr401`**, **`rateLimit`**, server-only **`OPENAI_API_KEY`**, prompts from **`buildSubmissionDraftAiPrompt.ts`**); UI copy states case details are sent to **OpenAI**; AI output is **review-only**, nothing filed; **no** DB writes, schema migrations, embedded browser, or filing automation for AI; destination selector from current justice destinations; **“I reviewed this draft”** before **Continue to action plan** → **`/justice/plan`**), per-destination prep pages, dedicated evidence page, saved cases, **`/justice/handling`** **Handling workbench** (§2 **Handling workbench — internal triage surface**), archived cases, packet (aggregate/export). **`/justice/plan`** links to **`/justice/preview`** from the **case packet** area. **`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **`/justice/chat-ai`** share **`src/lib/justice/commitIntakeToSessionAndServer.ts`** and **`src/lib/justice/normalizeCompanyWebsite.ts`** on form + scripted chat (optional company website: bare domains like `amazon.com` → `https://amazon.com`, sentinels like `none` / `n/a` → empty string). **Create commit (default):** **`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **new** **`/justice/chat-ai`** sessions — new case id, **`case_started`**, optional **`POST /api/justice/cases`**, **`intake_completed`**, then **`router.push("/justice/preview")`** (**`/justice/plan`** after preview continue). **Update commit:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** when an active case was hydrated (§2) — preserve case id/timeline, **`PATCH`** when signed in + UUID, no **`POST`**. **`/justice/chat`** and **`/justice/chat-ai`** use **`src/lib/justice/buildJusticeIntake.ts`** (**`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`**, **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`**, **`validateContactProofForIntake`**; §2). **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** powers AI turns on **`/justice/chat-ai`** (contract unchanged; §2).
- **Justice workspace hub (`/justice`):** **`/justice`** is shipped as a **thin**, **intentionally lightweight** Consumer Justice **workspace** landing — **not** a dashboard rewrite and **not** a replacement for **`/justice/plan`**. Copy explains that Surrenderless **organizes consumer issues into an action plan**, prepares **drafts, checklists, and records** for the user to use, and **does not file or submit complaints automatically**. Hub copy **recommends chat intake** and notes that **form intake** remains available for users who prefer the full structured form. **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** (single client mount **read-only**) renders the hub link list and, when **`readValidLocalJusticeIntake()`** finds valid **`sessionStorage`** intake, a compact **Current case** card — company name, category/product labels, submission-draft status from **`readTimeline`** using **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, and one primary link on the **Current case** card: **`/justice/preview`** when the submission draft is not reviewed; **`/justice/packet`** when the draft is reviewed but the prepared packet is not approved; **`/justice/plan`** when the draft is reviewed and the prepared packet is approved (§2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)**); the static **Continue current action plan** hub card is **omitted** in that case so the dynamic card is the only “next step” CTA. **Current case** display **re-refreshes client-side** when the **tab becomes visible** (`document.visibilityState === "visible"` on **`visibilitychange`**), when the **browser window regains focus** (`window` **`focus`**), and on **`storage`** (e.g. cross-tab updates to **`sessionStorage`** / shared storage) so the card is **less likely to stay stale** after **chat**, **preview**, **plan**, or other flows that mutate local intake/timeline — still using only **existing** local helpers (**`readValidLocalJusticeIntake`**, **`readTimeline`**, **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**); **no** hub case-list **`GET`**, **no** new routes, APIs, **`rules.ts`**, commit/preview/plan semantics, schemas, timeline event **definitions**, **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`**, or **`/justice/preview`** / **`/justice/plan`** behavior changes beyond their existing writes to **`sessionStorage`**. **Needs more info** chat routing on **Current case** — §2 **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**; compact **Current case** readiness checklist — §2 **Justice hub — Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`)**; approved next-step label + status on **Current case** — §2 **Justice hub — approved next-step label and status on Current case (`/justice`)**. With **no** local intake, link cards are **Start with chat intake** (**`/justice/chat-ai`**), **Use step-by-step chat** (**`/justice/chat`**; §2), **Continue current action plan**, **Start with form intake**, **Saved cases**. **No** case-list **`GET`**, **no** session mutation from the hub (reads only; active-case evidence **`GET`** for chat routing — §2 **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**). **`src/app/components/Header.tsx`** global nav order is **Justice** → **Chat intake** (**`/justice/chat-ai`**) → **Consumer case** (form intake → **`/justice/intake`**). **No** case **`GET`** on the hub, **no** duplication of **`rules.ts`** / plan readiness / destination logic, **no** new APIs, **no** auth changes, **no** schema or new DB tables, **no** automation, **no** filing or government submission from this surface. **Hub/header ordering** for chat-first entry is **UI-only** on this surface (see next bullet). **Preview-first intake finish** (**`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **`/justice/chat-ai`** → **`/justice/preview`**) is documented in §5; hub remains **read-only** (no commit from hub). **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** **create** vs **update** modes: §2 **Chat AI intake — hydrate & update commit**.
- **Justice hub — handling requested on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** — **read-only**, **session-only** (with §2 **Justice hub — approved next-step label and status on Current case (`/justice`)**). When valid local intake exists and **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** has **`handling_requested_at`** for **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`** (via **`readSessionApprovedNextAction`** — §2 **Approved next action shared state helpers**), the **Current case** card shows **Surrenderless handling requested** with recorded time; when **`handling_request_note`** is also in session, shows the note read-only (**`ApprovedNextActionHandlingRequestNoteReadOnly`**); when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is in session, shows **Acknowledged {time} — internal tracking triage only** (**`ApprovedNextActionHandlingAcknowledgedReadOnly`**); when **`handling_requested_at`** is in session, **display-only derived queue status** via **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingQueueStatusReadOnly`** (§2 **Justice hub — display-only derived handling queue status**) and **View in handling workbench** → **`/justice/handling`** appear below the **Current case** card (outside the plan/preview card link — §2 **Handling workbench — active-case back-link from hub**). When **`handling_requested_at`** is absent, **no** queue status line and **no** workbench link. **In-app tracking only** copy — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone. **No** server case **`GET`**, **no** request/clear buttons, **no** routing changes. Refreshes on **focus**, **`storage`**, and **visibility** like the existing snapshot. **No** schema, migration, API route, queue worker, filing record, timeline **type**, or automation.
- **Justice hub — display-only derived handling queue status (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** (**`ApprovedNextActionHandlingQueueStatusReadOnly`**, **`deriveHandlingQueueDisplayStatus`**) — **visibility-only** slice completing **queue-status parity** across every surface that shows handling (with §2 **Saved cases — handling requested visibility on All cases cards**, **Handling workbench — internal triage surface**, **Packet — display-only derived handling queue status**, **Chat AI intake — display-only derived handling queue status**, and **Plan — display-only derived handling queue status**). When the **Current case** snapshot has **`handlingRequestedAt`** / **`handling_requested_at`** (session **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** via **`readSessionApprovedNextAction`**), renders **display-only derived queue status** from existing **`handling_requested_at`** and **`handling_acknowledged_at`** / **`handlingAcknowledgedAt`** only (**no** new persisted field, **no** writes): **Queue status: Awaiting internal triage.** when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is absent; **Queue status: Acknowledged for internal tracking triage only** when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is set. Placed below the **Current case** card (after in-card handling disclaimer content) and before **View in handling workbench** (§2 **Handling workbench — active-case back-link from hub**). When **`handling_requested_at`** is absent, **no** queue status line. **Does not** change **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, request/ack/note behavior, server **`GET`**, plan/preview CTA, chat-intake hub cards, hub refresh, or workbench link. **In-app tracking only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, **`justice_case_filings`** row, timeline **type**, browser automation, filing automation, external submission/contact/queue automation, or **`/api/submit-form`**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued externally, or contacted automatically.
- **Justice hub — handled/open handling triage note on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** — **copy-only** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — handling requested on Current case**, **Justice hub — display-only derived handling queue status**, **Approved next action — centralized handled/open handling triage note copy**, **Saved cases — handled/open handling triage note on All cases cards**). When the session **Current case** snapshot has **`handling_requested_at`**, no **`handling_acknowledged_at`**, and **`approved_next_action.status === "completed"`** (via **`readSessionApprovedNextAction`** — **`showHandledOpenHandlingTriageNote`**), renders **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingHandledOpenTriageNote`** with variant **`redirect`** below **display-only** queue status and above **View in handling workbench**. **Hidden** when **`status !== "completed"`**, when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is set, or when **`handling_requested_at`** is absent. **No** **Mark acknowledged** on the hub. **Does not** change queue status, workbench link, session-only read model, focus/**`visibilitychange`**/**`storage`** refresh, in-card handling display, or external-action behavior. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, timeline **type**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only — **UI/navigation** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`)**, §2 **Saved cases — Needs more info chat routing CTA (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — hydrate & update commit**). When valid local intake exists (**Current case** card), uses **`isBasicCaseInfoReadyForEscalation`** from **`caseReadiness.ts`** on session intake (**no** predicate changes). When signed in and **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`** is a **UUID**, **`GET /api/justice/evidence?case_id={id}`** (same contract as saved cases/plan — **no** new API) on mount/focus/**`visibilitychange`**/**`storage`** refresh alongside the existing snapshot refresh; array length → saved proof/evidence count. Directly **below** the primary **Current case** preview/plan link (outside the nested card link), one outline secondary **`Link`**: when **`!isBasicCaseInfoReadyForEscalation(intake)`** — **Update in chat** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; when basics are complete, evidence count is loaded, and **`< 1`** — **Add proof in chat** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; when ready (**basics** + at least one saved item) — **no** extra CTA. Active session case only — **no** **`activateCaseInSession`**. Primary **Current case** nested card target — §2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)** (checklist inline links **unchanged**). Handling blocks below the card, hub link list, saved cases, plan, chat-ai, APIs, schema, and shared readiness logic **unchanged**. **Does not** claim filing, submission, contact, queueing, upload, storage, or automatic action by Surrenderless. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Justice hub — Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only — **UI/navigation** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**, §2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)**, §2 **Justice hub — Current case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice`)**, §2 **Saved cases — compact readiness checklist on All cases cards (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Saved cases — All cases prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Saved cases — Open case funnel routing (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — active case compact readiness checklist (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — active case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist proof CTA (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist basics CTA (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist draft-review CTA (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist prepared packet reviewed row (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness approved-next visibility (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Packet — prepared packet approval checkpoint (`/justice/packet`)**). When **Current case** exists, adds compact **`<ul>`** under the primary card link and **before** existing secondary **Update in chat** / **Add proof in chat** buttons — mirrors plan **Case readiness** clarity on the hub entry surface. Uses **existing** state only (**no** new API, **no** schema): **`basicsReady`** from **`isBasicCaseInfoReadyForEscalation`** on session intake; **`evidenceCount`** after **`!evidenceLoading`** (same evidence **`GET`** as §2 **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**); **`snapshot.reviewed`** from session **`readTimeline`** / **`submission_draft_reviewed`**. Three rows: **Basic case info: yes/not yet** — when **`snapshot && !basicsReady`**, inline **Update in chat** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; **Evidence: yes/not yet** (or **Evidence: loading...** while **`evidenceLoading`**) — when loaded and **`(evidenceCount ?? 0) < 1`**, inline **Add proof in chat** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; **Submission draft reviewed: yes/not yet** — when **`snapshot && !snapshot.reviewed`**, inline **Review submission draft** → **`/justice/preview`**; fourth row when draft reviewed — §2 **Justice hub — Current case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice`)**. Same inline link classes as plan checklist CTAs (**`hubChecklistLinkCls`**). **Does not** change **`showUpdateInChat`**, **`showAddProofInChat`**, primary **Current case** card **`href`** / label (§2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)**), evidence fetch, handling blocks, or hub link list. **Does not** claim filing, submission, contact, queueing, upload, storage, or automatic action by Surrenderless. **No** API, schema, helper, plan, preview, chat-ai, or cases changes on this slice. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Justice hub — Current case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only — **UI/navigation** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`)**, §2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — active case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Saved cases — All cases prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist prepared packet reviewed row (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Packet — prepared packet approval checkpoint (`/justice/packet`)**, §2 **Plan — prepared packet approval surfaced (`/justice/plan`)**). Adds page-local **`STORAGE_PREPARED_PACKET_APPROVED_V1`** and **`readSessionPreparedPacketApproved(caseId)`** (same JSON map pattern as preview/plan/chat-ai). Extends **`readSnapshotFromLocalSession`** / **`CurrentCaseSnapshot`** with **`packetApproved: readSessionPreparedPacketApproved(caseId)`** when **`caseId`** exists — refreshed on existing **`refreshHubState`** (focus/**`storage`**/**`visibilitychange`** — **no** new listeners). In **Current case** compact checklist **`<ul>`**, **after** **Submission draft reviewed**, **only when** **`snapshot.reviewed`**: **Prepared case packet reviewed: yes** when **`packetApproved`**; **Prepared case packet reviewed: not yet** with inline **Review prepared case packet** → **`/justice/packet`** when not approved (**`hubChecklistLinkCls`**). **Navigation/readiness only** — closes hub recovery gap between draft review and packet approval (parity with chat-ai). **Does not** change evidence **`GET`**, handling blocks, approved-next labels, **Update in chat** / **Add proof in chat**, primary card **`href`** / **`primaryLabel`** (§2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)**), routes, APIs, schema, handlers, or shared libs. **Session-only** for packet approval on hub (**no** case **`GET`** on this slice). **In-app tracking only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, or contacted anyone. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, browser automation, filing automation, or timeline **type**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued externally, uploaded, stored, or contacted automatically.
- **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only — **UI/navigation** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`)**, §2 **Justice hub — Current case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — active case banner work-link funnel routing (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Plan — prepared next action after draft review (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Preview — Continue routes to packet when prepared packet not approved (`/justice/preview`)**, §2 **Saved cases — Open case funnel routing (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Packet — prepared packet approval checkpoint (`/justice/packet`)**). Page-local **`primaryHref`** and **`primaryLabel`** on the nested **Current case** primary **`Link`**: when **`!snapshot.reviewed`** — **`/justice/preview`**, **Continue to submission preview**; when **`snapshot.reviewed && !snapshot.packetApproved`** — **`/justice/packet`**, **Review prepared case packet**; when **`snapshot.reviewed && snapshot.packetApproved`** — **`/justice/plan`**, **Continue to action plan**. Uses existing **`snapshot.reviewed`** (session **`readTimeline`** / **`submission_draft_reviewed`**) and **`snapshot.packetApproved`** (**`readSessionPreparedPacketApproved`** — §2 **Justice hub — Current case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice`)**) — **no** new API, **no** schema. Aligns default hub card click with post-draft funnel (packet before plan when packet not yet approved). Checklist **`<ul>`**, prepared-packet row, approved-next lines, handling blocks, evidence **`GET`**, **`showUpdateInChat`**, **`showAddProofInChat`**, static hub link list, routes beyond the three targets above, APIs, schema, handlers, filing/submission/contact/queue/upload/storage/automatic-action behavior **unchanged**. **Navigation/readiness only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, or contacted anyone. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Justice hub — approved next-step label and status on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only — **visibility-only** slice (with §2 **Saved cases — approved next-step label on All cases cards (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Saved cases — Needs attention approved-next-action label alignment (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Saved cases — Needs attention approved-next step label visibility (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness approved-next visibility (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — approved next-step label/status on Active case banner (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — Recap current-action label alignment (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Approved next action shared state helpers**). In **`readSnapshotFromLocalSession`**, reuses existing **`approvedNext`** from **`readSessionApprovedNextAction(caseId)`** (**`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** — §2 **Approved next action shared state helpers**); derives **`stepLabel`** from **`approvedNext?.label?.trim()`** and **`statusLabel`** from **`approvedNextActionStatusLabel(approvedNext?.status)`** (**Approved** / **Started** / **Handled**). On the **Current case** card (inside the primary **`Link`** — §2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)** — after **Submission draft reviewed** / **not reviewed** and **before** in-card handling lines and **`{primaryLabel}`**), shows read-only **Next step: {label}** (bold **label**) when **`stepLabel`** exists and **Approved next action: {statusLabel}** when **`statusLabel`** exists — small neutral **`text-xs`** styling aligned with hub card copy. **Does not** add **Open {label}**, **Record action handled**, refresh, **`GET`**, **`PATCH`**, or server **`client_state`** read on the hub. Readiness checklist, **Update in chat** / **Add proof in chat** CTAs, **display-only** handling queue status below the card, **View in handling workbench**, hub link list, Plan, Packet, Chat AI, Cases, APIs, and schema **unchanged** on this slice. **In-app tracking visibility only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, contacted anyone, uploaded, stored files, or taken automatic action on the user's behalf. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, browser automation, filing automation, or timeline **type**.
- **Justice workspace recovery routing (`/justice` fallback):** When a Consumer Justice page **cannot hydrate or resume a usable active case** (e.g. no valid local intake and **no server row** after **`GET /api/justice/cases`**, plan **GET**/list **hydrate** failures / empty list, **`useJusticeActionPageHydration`** unable to hydrate, or analogous **missing `STORAGE_CASE_ID` / intake** escapes on routed surfaces aligned with this pattern), **`router.replace("/justice")`** or **`router.push("/justice")`** (**and matching `Link` destinations** where the same UX intent applies) lands the user on the **`/justice`** workspace hub — the **recovery hub** for missing / **no-case** / **failed-resume** states (replacing earlier **`/justice/intake`**-only redirects for those outcomes). **`/justice`** preserves **chat-first recovery** (**Start with chat intake** is first on the hub) while **`Start with form intake`** stays one click away. **Routing / copy-only** slice: **no** changes to **`rules.ts`**, recommendation logic, destination ordering, schemas, **API** route implementations (handlers, payloads, responses), auth guards, **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** or other **persistence**/session commit behavior, timeline event **semantics**, **`/justice/preview`** deterministic or AI-assisted draft **generation**, filing automation, or filing/submission flows.
- **Chat-first navigation promotion (UI only on hub/header):** **`/justice`** workspace and **`Header.tsx`** emphasize **AI conversational chat intake** first — **Justice** → **Chat intake** (**`/justice/chat-ai`**) → **Consumer case** (**`/justice/intake`**) in the header; **Start with chat intake** is the **first** hub card (**`/justice/chat-ai`**). A second hub card, **Use step-by-step chat**, links to **scripted** **`/justice/chat`** (§2 **Justice hub — step-by-step chat fallback**). **`/justice/chat`** remains **scripted** Q&A (not LLM-driven); **scripted chat behavior is unchanged** on this slice. **`/justice/chat-ai`** page copy presents conversational intake as the primary **Your consumer case** path (not a separate “prototype” label). **Preview-first intake finish:** after successful commit, **`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **`/justice/chat-ai`** **`router.push`** **`/justice/preview`**; after successful draft review on preview, **Continue** routes to **`/justice/packet`** when the prepared packet is not approved and **`/justice/plan`** when it is (§2 **Preview — Continue routes to packet when prepared packet not approved (`/justice/preview`)**); users can also reach **`/justice/plan`** via hub, packet, or other surfaces (**`submission_draft_reviewed`** tracking unchanged). **Navigation slice only:** **no** new APIs, **no** prompt/parser changes, **no** LLM behavior changes, **no** auth changes on scripted chat, **no** schema or DB changes, **no** Supabase changes, **no** **`caseReadiness.ts`** changes, **no** plan **`rules.ts`** logic changes, **no** preview/plan behavior changes beyond existing flows. (Intake **commit** and **hydration** behavior for **`/justice/chat-ai`** are documented in §2 **Chat AI intake — hydrate & update commit**.)
- **Chat intake — shared `JusticeIntake` builder (scripted `/justice/chat` + AI `/justice/chat-ai` + structured alignment):** **`src/lib/justice/buildJusticeIntake.ts`** centralizes **`BuildJusticeIntakeParts`** defaults and conversion: **`defaultBuildJusticeIntakeParts()`**, forward **`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`** (trim strings, **`normalizeCompanyWebsite`** on scripted/AI paths that use it, merge **`money_amount`** + **`desired_resolution`** into **`money_involved`** with separator **` — Desired outcome: `**, contact fields only when **`already_contacted === "yes"`**, optional **`consumer_us_state`**), and reverse **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** (hydrate saved **`JusticeIntake`** from **`sessionStorage`** — conservative split of **`money_involved`** on that separator or hyphen variant, safe contact enums, **`already_contacted`** only **`yes`** when stored as yes). **Scripted** **`/justice/chat`** and **AI** **`/justice/chat-ai`** both produce the **same `JusticeIntake`** shape before commit. **`parseIntakeChatAiResponse.ts`** imports shared **`defaultBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** (re-exported) instead of duplicating defaults. **Post-intake rail:** build intake → **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** (**`create`** or **`update`** on chat-ai when applicable) → **`/justice/preview`** → **`/justice/plan`**. **Still unchanged on this slice:** **`rules.ts`**, readiness, preview draft **generation**, filing/evidence APIs, Supabase schema, **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** contract, auto-filing/submission automation (§1).
- **Chat intake — shared contact-proof validation (scripted `/justice/chat` + AI `/justice/chat-ai`):** **`validateContactProofForIntake`** in **`src/lib/justice/buildJusticeIntake.ts`** (same module as the builder): when **`already_contacted === "yes"`**, **`contact_proof_type`** **`none`** or **`ticket`** requires non-empty **`contact_proof_text`** with fixed error strings (**“Describe your contact attempt before continuing.”** / **“Enter the ticket or case number before continuing.”**). Used by **scripted** chat and **AI** chat before commit (**`create`** or **`update`**). **Validation rules unchanged** on hydrate/update slice; **no** change to **`rules.ts`**, readiness, preview draft **generation**, or intake-chat API.
- **AI intake chat API (`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`):** **`src/app/api/justice/intake-chat/route.ts`** with **`buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`** and **`parseIntakeChatAiResponse.ts`**. **Request:** `{ user_message, parts: BuildJusticeIntakeParts, conversation_history?: { role: "user" | "assistant"; content: string }[] }` — one user turn plus current partial parts and optional capped history. **Response:** `{ assistantMessage, parts }` — updated **`BuildJusticeIntakeParts`** (pre-commit; not full **`JusticeIntake`** until client runs **`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`**). **Security:** same envelope as **`preview-draft`** — **`getUserOr401`**, **`rateLimit`**, **`OPENAI_API_KEY`** server-only, bounded body, JSON validation/clamping, OpenAI **`json_object`** response parsed before return. **No** Supabase / DB writes, **no** timeline writes, **no** case creation, **no** **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** in the API. Consumed by **`/justice/chat-ai`** (§2). **Scripted `/justice/chat`** unchanged.
- **AI chat intake (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** — **primary AI conversational intake** UI (hub/header **Chat intake** and **Start with chat intake** → here; plan **Update in chat** → here; §2 **Chat-first navigation promotion** / **Justice-wide navigation alignment**). **Separate route** from **scripted** **`/justice/chat`** (scripted page **unchanged**; linked as **Use step-by-step chat**). **`/justice/intake`** remains the **structured form fallback** (**Edit structured form**). **Clerk** sign-in required (**`JusticeActionResumeSignInPrompt`** when signed out). On mount, **`readValidLocalJusticeIntake()`** (§2 **hydrate & update commit**): if valid **`STORAGE_INTAKE`** exists, **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** seeds **`parts`**, **Recap** shows the loaded case immediately, assistant copy explains the case is loaded and the user can describe changes; otherwise fresh **`defaultBuildJusticeIntakeParts()`** + new-case greeting. When **`isUpdatingExistingCase`**, compact **Active case** banner above the main chat card with compact readiness checklist and funnel-aware footer work links (§2 **Chat AI intake — active case context banner (Update in chat)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — active case compact readiness checklist (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — active case banner work-link funnel routing (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**); session changes surface in **Updated in this chat** and/or folded into **What happens next** when Continue handoff is visible (§2 **Chat AI intake — session change summary (Update in chat)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — Continue handoff session-change integration (Update in chat)**). When **`approved_next_action`** is present, **Current action tracking** in **Recap** with funnel-aware footer work links matching the **Active case** banner (§2 **Chat AI intake — Recap current-action work-link funnel routing (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**). Local **`messages`** and **`parts`**; each send calls **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** with **`{ user_message, parts, conversation_history }`** (history = prior UI messages only; in-flight send guard §2; API error-copy polish §2). Shows assistant replies, compact **Recap** (including **Proof / evidence** guidance §2 and **Current action tracking** when applicable), OpenAI disclosure. **Continue to submission preview** blocked until basics present (§2 preview-readiness polish); **evidence not required** before preview. When complete: **`validateContactProofForIntake`** → **`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`** → **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** with **`mode: "update"`** when hydrated from an existing case, else **`create`** (**`commitLogLabel`**: **`justice chat-ai`**) → **`/justice/preview`** → **`/justice/plan`**. **Not filing automation** — same review/preview/plan rail as before. **Unchanged:** **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** contract, prompt/parser, **`rules.ts`**, readiness, preview draft **generation**, filing/evidence **APIs**, Supabase schema, scripted **`/justice/chat`** Q&A.
- **Chat AI intake — proof/evidence guidance (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** only — **UI/copy** slice in the **Recap** block (near **Continue to submission preview**). **Proof / evidence** panel explains that as the case is built **in this chat**, Surrenderless can organize proof such as **screenshots, receipts, order confirmations, emails, account pages, tracking pages, call notes, and chat transcripts** to strengthen the case. Copy frames this as the **chat-first workflow** (next step in the same case), not a separate manual detour. On **Update in chat** with a server-backed **UUID** case, a collapsed **Add a proof note** form can save one metadata row in-app with required **title** + **evidence_type** and optional **evidence date** / **description** (§2 **Chat AI intake — add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**); on **fresh intake** (before first server-backed UUID case), the same form can **stage** metadata locally until **Continue to submission preview** (§2 **Chat AI intake — staged proof notes on fresh intake (Proof / evidence panel)**); when saved rows exist, a collapsed **Recent proof notes** block shows up to **3** metadata rows with inline **Edit** and **Delete** (§2 **Chat AI intake — recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**); client-side **proof keyword nudge** after chat send may point users to **Add a proof note** and **prefill empty** title/description from the triggering message (§2 **Chat AI intake — proof keyword nudge in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**); preview shows title, type, optional date, truncated description — **no** **`source_url`** / **`storage_note`** in chat. CTA **Organize evidence** → **`/justice/evidence`** (existing **`justice_case_evidence`** surface: title, type, optional date, description, optional **`source_url`** / **`storage_note`** — **metadata/notes/links only**; **file uploads are not available**; full list/edit/delete). **Evidence is optional before preview**; saving at least one item helps before **escalation/submission** (plan **ready to escalate** still uses evidence count §2); **nothing is filed automatically** from the app yet. **No** **`justice_case_evidence`** rows auto-created from chat; **no** evidence on **`BuildJusticeIntakeParts`**; **Continue** / commit (**create** / **update**) unchanged. **No** API, Supabase schema, **`rules.ts`**, **`caseReadiness.ts`**, preview generation, commit semantics, filing behavior, or intake-chat contract changes. Shown for **fresh intake** and **hydrated Update in chat**. - **Chat AI intake — saved evidence count in Recap (Proof / evidence panel) (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** only — **chat-first visibility** slice (with §2 **Chat AI intake — proof/evidence guidance**). When **Update in chat** is active (**`isUpdatingExistingCase`**) and the user is signed in with a **UUID** **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, page-local **`loadSavedEvidencePreview`** calls existing **`GET /api/justice/evidence?case_id={id}`** (same pattern as **`/justice/plan`** saved-evidence preview and **`/justice/cases`** progress fetch — **no** new route, **no** schema) and sets **`savedEvidenceCount`** plus **`recentEvidenceRows`** (up to 3 newest — §2 **Chat AI intake — recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**). - **Chat AI intake — add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel) (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** only — **chat-first capture** slice (with §2 **Chat AI intake — proof/evidence guidance**, **Chat AI intake — saved evidence count in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — edit recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — proof keyword nudge in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**). Submit **`POST /api/justice/evidence`** with **`case_id`**, **`title`**, **`evidence_type`**, and **`evidence_date`** / **`description`** only when trimmed non-empty — **no** new API, **no** schema; server appends **`evidence_added`** timeline via existing route. On **Update in chat**, requires signed-in **UUID** **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`** (**`canAddProofNoteInChat`**). - **Chat AI intake — staged proof notes on fresh intake (Proof / evidence panel) (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/stagedProofNotes.ts`** — **client-side staging** slice (with §2 **Chat AI intake — add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**). - **Chat AI intake — hydrate & update commit:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** is the in-app **Update in chat** path for an **active local case** (e.g. from **`/justice/plan`**, **Saved cases**, or hub — §2 **Saved cases — Needs more info chat routing CTA (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**). **Hydration:** one-time mount read via **`readValidLocalJusticeIntake()`** → **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** in **`buildJusticeIntake.ts`** (shared with scripted/structured alignment); baseline **`parts`** snapshot for session change summary — §2 **Chat AI intake — session change summary (Update in chat)**. **Active case** orientation banner when hydrated — §2 **Chat AI intake — active case context banner (Update in chat)**; compact readiness checklist on **Update in chat** — §2 **Chat AI intake — active case compact readiness checklist (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — active case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**; funnel-aware footer work links on **Active case** banner — §2 **Chat AI intake — active case banner work-link funnel routing (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**; same funnel-aware footer work links on **Recap → Current action tracking** when **`approvedNextAction`** exists — §2 **Chat AI intake — Recap current-action work-link funnel routing (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**; read-only approved next-step label/status on **Active case** banner when **`approvedNextAction`** exists — §2 **Chat AI intake — approved next-step label/status on Active case banner (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**. **Commit:** **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** **`mode: "update"`** preserves **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, does **not** call **`newCaseId()`**, does **not** **`clearTimelineForNewCase`**, does **not** append **`case_started`**, does **not** clear FTC/mock keys, does **not** fire **`intake_completed`**, does **not** **`POST /api/justice/cases`**; writes **`STORAGE_INTAKE`**; when signed in and case id is a **UUID**, **`PATCH /api/justice/cases/[id]`** with `{ intake, timeline }` (same pattern as merchant save). **Create** **`mode`** (default) unchanged for new intake and for **`/justice/intake`** / **`/justice/chat`**. **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** returns **`CommitIntakeResult`** **`{ caseId, serverPersisted }`** — **create** sets **`serverPersisted`** when signed-in **`POST /api/justice/cases`** succeeds with **`id`**; **update** sets **`serverPersisted`** when **`PATCH`** succeeds (callers may ignore; §2 **Chat AI intake — staged proof notes on fresh intake (Proof / evidence panel)** uses it before flushing staged proof). **No** new timeline event type for “intake updated” on this slice. **Limitations:** **`/justice/intake`** submit still uses **create** only (editing loaded session can still spawn a duplicate case — pre-existing); signed-out or non-UUID session ids get local intake update only (no server PATCH); **no** filing/submission automation.

Prevents rapid **double-click** / fast **Enter** from starting overlapping **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** requests (stale **`conversation_history`**, duplicate bubbles, last-writer **`parts`**). **Normal send** unchanged; **failed-request retry** still works after the request finishes; **Recap** / preview-readiness / **Continue** → **`/justice/preview`** behavior unchanged. **Page-only reliability**: **no** API, prompt/parser, **`buildJusticeIntake.ts`**, commit helper, preview/plan, routing/hub/header, schemas, Supabase, readiness, **`rules.ts`**, or scripted **`/justice/chat`** changes.
- **AI chat intake — API error-copy polish (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** only — page-local **`formatIntakeChatApiError(status, serverError)`** in **`handleSend`**: for **`!res.ok`** responses, replaces raw server **`error`** strings (e.g. **`Unauthorized`**, **`Invalid model JSON`**, **`OPENAI_API_KEY not configured`**) with clearer user-facing retry guidance — **401** (session expired, sign in and resend), **429** (wait and retry), **502** (usable AI reply), **500** (including missing-key vs generic server error), **400**, **413** / too-large body, and a generic fallback. **Success path**, **input** clearing on success, **retry** after failure (input/messages/**`parts`** preserved), **duplicate-send** guard, **Recap**, and **Continue** → **`/justice/preview`** unchanged. - **AI intake — `purchase_or_signup` extraction (`buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`):** **Issue found:** on **`/justice/chat-ai`**, a user said a **“phone case”** never arrived; the assistant repeated “phone case” in **`assistantMessage`** but returned **`parts.purchase_or_signup`** empty, so the recap **Product / service** line stayed blank and the pre-preview basics gate blocked. **Fix (prompt-only):** **`src/lib/justice/buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`** now explicitly instructs the model to populate **`purchase_or_signup`** whenever the product, service, order item, subscription, account, charge target, or thing purchased/charged is **clearly stated** (with examples such as phone case, Prime, checking account, internet plan) — without inventing when unstated. **No** change to **`parseIntakeChatAiResponse.ts`**, **`/justice/chat-ai`** page, API route behavior, commit helper, preview/plan, or scripted chat. **Smoke-tested:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** now maps **“phone case”** into **Product / service** and a complete intake reaches **`/justice/preview`**.

In the existing top approval / prepared-action area (when framing is active and the packet is already approved), **`status === "started"`** shows **Next action started**, **Opened for next step**, and copy that the approved in-app step was opened (with stored **label** when present); post-approval emerald card uses **`getApprovedPacketNextStepExplainer`** **started** variant with **action plan or chat intake** record-handled guidance (§2 **Packet — post-approval approved-step explainer and emerald card copy refresh (`/justice/packet`)**, §2 **Packet — started-state record-handled copy alignment (`/justice/packet`)**); **`status === "approved"`** keeps prior **Packet approved for next action** wording and **Open {label}** CTA with in-app prep/tracking clarifier (§2 **Packet — post-approval approved-step explainer and emerald card copy refresh (`/justice/packet`)**; started write on click — §2 **Packet — Open approved step marks started tracking (`/justice/packet`)**). **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, browser automation, filing automation, or timeline **type**; **no** changes to case summary, timeline, evidence, **`JusticeFilingRecords`**, **`JusticeCaseTasks`**, copy/download/print, or the packet approval checkbox flow; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, or contacted automatically. Keeps **packet** aligned with **plan** in **prepare → approve → start/track** (§2 **Approved next action started** on plan).
- **Packet — started-state record-handled copy alignment (`/justice/packet`):** **`src/app/justice/packet/page.tsx`** only — **copy-only** slice (with §2 **Packet — post-approval approved-step explainer and emerald card copy refresh (`/justice/packet`)**, §2 **Packet — approved next action started surfaced (`/justice/packet`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — record action handled in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**). When **`approved_next_action.status === "started"`**, started-state guidance no longer says record handled **from your action plan when ready** alone: page-local **`getApprovedPacketNextStepExplainer`** **started** branch and duplicate inline started-state copy in the post-approval explainer (and matching inner-card started branch) now say **from your action plan or chat intake when ready** — aligned with chat **Record action handled for now** (§2 **Chat AI intake — record action handled in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**) and existing handling/workbench **action plan or chat intake** wording. **Does not** change **`handleApprovedNextActionOpen`**, **`handleApprovePreparedPacket`**, hydrate, **`persistApprovedNextActionClientState`**, routing, buttons, Open/Link behavior, Plan, Chat AI, Hub, Cases, APIs, schema, or state handling. **In-app tracking only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, or contacted anyone. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, browser automation, filing automation, or timeline **type**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued externally, or contacted automatically.

When the packet is approved and **`approved_next_action.status`** is **`"approved"`** (not **`started`** or **`completed`**), **Open {label}** in the **Packet approved for next action** inner card is a **`<button>`** calling page-local **`handleApprovedNextActionOpen`**: builds **`approved_next_action`** with existing **`label`** / **`href`**, sets **`status: "started"`** and **`started_at`** (preserves **`approved_at`**), merges tracking fields via **`mergeApprovedNextActionTrackingFields`**, writes **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** and **`justice_prepared_packet_approved_v1`** session maps, updates React state, **`await`**s page-local **`persistApprovedNextActionClientState`** (**`GET` + **`mergeClientStateWithApprovedNextAction`** + **`PATCH`** existing **`/api/justice/cases/[id]`** **`client_state`**) for signed-in **UUID** cases, then **`router.push`** to the approved **`href`**. If already **`completed`**, navigates only — **no** status downgrade. When **`started`** or **`completed`**, **Open {label}** remains plain **`Link`** navigation — **does not** downgrade **`started`** → **`approved`** or **`completed`** to a lower state. **Does not** change approval checkpoint, **`handleApprovePreparedPacket`**, post-approval explainer copy, **`showPreparedActionPacketFraming`** gates, packet body, copy/download/print, **`JusticeFilingRecords`**, **`JusticeCaseTasks`**, prep routes, APIs, schema, **`rules.ts`**, plan, preview, chat-ai, hub, cases. **In-app tracking only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, or contacted anyone. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, browser automation, filing automation, or timeline **type**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued externally, or contacted automatically.

- **Approved next action target (`client_state` — packet + plan):** **`src/lib/justice/types.ts`** (**`JusticeApprovedNextAction`**, **`approved_next_action`** on **`JusticeCaseClientState`**), **`src/app/justice/packet/page.tsx`**, **`src/app/justice/plan/page.tsx`**. - **Approved next action shared state helpers (`approvedNextActionState.ts`):** **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionState.ts`** centralizes **`approved_next_action`** parsing from unknown **`client_state`** / session values (**`parseApprovedNextAction`**, **`parseApprovedNextActionFromClientState`**, **`parseJusticeCaseClientState`**), status display labels (**`approvedNextActionStatusLabel`** — **Approved** / **Started** / **Handled**), handling awaiting-triage membership (**`isHandlingAwaitingTriageApprovedNextAction`** — §2 **Approved next action — shared handling awaiting-triage membership predicate**), follow-up clearing (**`clearFollowUpFromApprovedNextAction`** — removes **`follow_up_needed`** while preserving **`outcome_note`**, **`follow_up_at`**, **`handling_requested_at`**, **`handling_request_note`**, **`handling_acknowledged_at`**, **`status`**, **`href`**, **`label`**, **`approved_at`**, **`started_at`**, **`completed_at`**, and other fields), handling-request note updates (**`applyHandlingRequestNoteToApprovedNextAction`** — sets or clears **`handling_request_note`** only), cleared-follow-up **`client_state`** merge (**`mergeClientStateWithClearedFollowUp`** — preserves **`prepared_packet_approved`**), plan/packet persist merge (**`mergeClientStateWithApprovedNextAction`** — preserves prior fields unless incoming action omits **`handling_request_note`** intentionally; forces **`prepared_packet_approved`** on plan persist), session + server resolve (**`resolveApprovedNextAction`** — merges **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** with **`client_state`**; **does not downgrade** **`completed`** → **`started`** → **`approved`**), display hydrate (**`hydrateApprovedNextActionForDisplay`** — coalesces **`handling_acknowledged_at`** from session, resolved action, and raw **`client_state`** for plan/chat/packet UI), tracking-field preserve on persist (**`mergeApprovedNextActionTrackingFields`** — keeps **`handling_requested_at`** / **`handling_acknowledged_at`** when a patch omits them), and session map read/write (**`STORAGE_APPROVED_NEXT_ACTION_V1`** / **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`**). **`/justice/chat-ai`**, **`/justice/cases`**, **`/justice/plan`**, and **`/justice/packet`** import these helpers (chat-ai **Current action tracking** / **Open {label}** when **`approved`** / **Record action handled for now** / **completed-step clarity** / **Mark follow-up handled** / **Request Surrenderless handling** / **Mark acknowledged** — §2 **Chat AI intake — approved next action display hydrate**, **Chat AI intake — Open approved step marks started in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, **Chat AI intake — record action handled in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, **Chat AI intake — completed-step clarity in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, **Chat AI intake — handling requested in Current action tracking**, **Chat AI intake — acknowledge handling request in Current action tracking**; cases **Needs attention** / **Clear follow-up** / **All cases** **`CaseApprovedNextActionTracking`** — **Next step: {label}** when set on **All cases** (§2 **Saved cases — approved next-step label on All cases cards**) and on **Needs attention** handling-request and follow-up cards (§2 **Saved cases — Needs attention approved-next step label visibility (`/justice/cases`)**), **`handling_requested_at`** visibility (§2 **Saved cases — handling requested visibility on All cases cards**); plan **approved** / **started** / **handled** / outcome follow-up / **Request Surrenderless handling** / **Mark acknowledged** persist (§2 **Plan — acknowledge handling request in Surrenderless handling UI**); packet **approval** hydrate and return-to-plan). Reduces duplicated parsing/resolving/merge logic across all four surfaces and keeps handling request/note/ack visible when session and server disagree. **No** schema, migration, API route, queue worker, automation, filing behavior, or timeline **type**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued, or contacted automatically. **No** schema, migration, API route, queue worker, automation, filing behavior, or timeline **type**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued, or contacted automatically.
